2026-05-05T12:13:41.6352840Z     data: list[dict[str, Any]] = json.load(open(path))
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6353414Z     return {f["fqname"]: f for f in data}
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6353786Z 
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6353800Z 
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6354040Z def required_positional(func: dict[str, Any]) -> int:
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6354625Z     """Count required positional arguments."""
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6355346Z     return sum(1 for a in func.get("positional", []) if not a.get("has_default"))
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6356210Z 
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6356228Z 
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6356487Z def total_positional(func: dict[str, Any]) -> int:
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6356862Z     """Count total positional arguments."""
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6357177Z     return len(func.get("positional", []))
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6357546Z 
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6357555Z 
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6357790Z def analyze(signatures_path: str, calls_path: str) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6358377Z     """Analyze runtime impact of signature changes.
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6359048Z 
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6359185Z     Args:
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6359578Z         signatures_path: Path to signatures JSON file.
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6360316Z         calls_path: Path to runtime calls JSON (dict of {func_name: count}).
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6360856Z 
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6360992Z     Returns:
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6361505Z         List of impact issue dictionaries with keys: function, risk, count.
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6362189Z     """
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6362398Z     funcs = load_funcs(signatures_path)
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6362670Z     try:
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6362921Z         runtime: dict[str, int] = json.load(open(calls_path))
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6363259Z     except Exception:
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6363477Z         runtime = {}
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6363620Z 
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6363720Z     issues: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6364097Z 
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6364330Z     for fqname, func in funcs.items():
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6364698Z         name = func.get("name", fqname.split(":")[-1])
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6365057Z         count = runtime.get(name, runtime.get(fqname, 0))
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6365401Z         min_args = required_positional(func)
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6365603Z 
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6365702Z         if min_args > 0 and count == 0:
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6366379Z             issues.append(
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6366805Z                 {
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6367162Z                     "function": fqname,
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6367616Z                     "risk": "UNKNOWN",
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6368307Z                     "change": "not observed at runtime",
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6368862Z                     "count": 0,
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6369283Z                 }
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6369558Z             )
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6369755Z         elif count > 0:
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6370085Z             issues.append(
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6370510Z                 {
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6370729Z                     "function": fqname,
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6371009Z                     "risk": "LOW",
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6371270Z                     "change": "observed",
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6371547Z                     "count": count,
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6371804Z                 }
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6372000Z             )
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6372111Z 
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6372198Z     return issues
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6372317Z 
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6372324Z 
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6372418Z if __name__ == "__main__":
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6372656Z     if len(sys.argv) < 3:
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6373029Z         print("Usage: python runtime_impact.py <signatures.json> <calls.json>")
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6373446Z         sys.exit(1)
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6373679Z     result = analyze(sys.argv[1], sys.argv[2])
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6373990Z     print(json.dumps(result, indent=2))
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6374257Z ```
2026-05-05T12:13:41.6374365Z

2026-05-05T12:13:49.3438854Z     ...
2026-05-05T12:13:49.3439064Z     ## Risk Model and Enforcement
2026-05-05T12:13:49.3439308Z     ...
2026-05-05T12:13:49.3439490Z     ### CI Enforcement
2026-05-05T12:13:49.3439693Z     
2026-05-05T12:13:49.3440052Z     The risk assessment is operationalized through `risk_gate.py` and `enforce_gate.py`:
2026-05-05T12:13:49.3440488Z     
2026-05-05T12:13:49.3441060Z     1. **Risk Gate Execution**: `risk_gate.py` contains the `run()` function which parses the diff and runtime data to generate a comprehensive `report.json`
2026-05-05T12:13:49.3441811Z     2. **Gate Enforcement**: `enforce_gate.py` consumes this report:
2026-05-05T12:13:49.3442362Z        - If any item is flagged as `HIGH` risk → exits with code `1` (blocks build)
2026-05-05T12:13:49.3442986Z        - If `UNKNOWN` risks are detected → issues a warning but allows build (exit code `0`)
2026-05-05T12:13:49.3443414Z     
2026-05-05T12:13:49.3443572Z     ---
2026-05-05T12:13:49.3443736Z     
2026-05-05T12:13:49.3443895Z     ...
2026-05-05T12:13:49.3444060Z     ````

2026-05-05T12:14:06.8013802Z     172. def cmd_check_commits(args: argparse.Namespace) -> int:
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8014565Z     173.     """Run ImpactGuard pipeline comparing two git commits."""
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8015259Z     174.     from .pipeline import run_pipeline_git
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8015788Z     175. 
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8016689Z     176.     print(f"Checking impact: {args.old_ref} → {args.new_ref}")

2026-05-05T12:14:06.8017637Z     178.     try:
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8018007Z     179.         result = run_pipeline_git(
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8018525Z     180.             old_ref=args.old_ref,
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8019011Z     181.             new_ref=args.new_ref,
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8019608Z     182.             files=args.files if hasattr(args, "files") else None,
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8020290Z     183.             runtime_path=args.runtime,
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8020829Z     184.             output_path=args.output,
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8021301Z     185.         )
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8021629Z     186. 
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8021987Z     187.         print(f"\n=== Comparison ===")
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8022579Z     188.         comparison = result.get("comparison", {})
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8023351Z     189.         print(f"Breaking changes: {len(comparison.get('breaking', []))}")
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8024315Z     190.         print(f"Non-breaking changes: {len(comparison.get('nonbreaking', []))}")
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8025043Z     191. 
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8025384Z     192.         if "risk" in result:
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8025873Z     193.             risk_items = result["risk"]
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8027007Z     194.             high = sum(1 for r in risk_items if r.get("risk") == "HIGH")
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8027751Z     195.             print(f"\n=== Risk Analysis ===")
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8028318Z     196.             print(f"HIGH risk: {high}")
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8028782Z     197. 
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8029184Z     198.         if "report_html" in result and args.output:
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8029823Z     199.             print(f"\nReport written to {args.output}")
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8030394Z     200. 
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8030700Z     201.         return 0
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8031059Z     202. 
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8031364Z     203.     except Exception as e:
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8031787Z     204.         print(f"Error: {e}")
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8032202Z     205.         return 1

2026-05-05T12:14:06.8033562Z     208. def cmd_install_hooks(args: argparse.Namespace) -> int:
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8034269Z     209.     """Install git hooks for ImpactGuard."""
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8034788Z     210.     import os
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8035163Z     211.     import stat
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8035531Z     212. 
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8035890Z     213.     repo_path = Path(args.repo_path)
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8036657Z     214.     git_dir = repo_path / ".git"
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8037121Z     215. 
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8037447Z     216.     if not git_dir.exists():
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8038037Z     217.         print(f"Error: Not a git repository: {repo_path}")
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8038643Z     218.         return 1
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8039004Z     219. 
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8039331Z     220.     hooks_dir = git_dir / "hooks"

2026-05-05T12:14:06.8040680Z     223.     # Determine which hooks to install
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8041560Z     224.     install_pre = args.pre or args.both or (not args.pre and not args.post and not args.both)
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8042769Z     225.     install_post = args.post or args.both or (not args.pre and not args.post and not args.both)
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8043602Z     226. 
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8043961Z     227.     # Get the impactguard command path
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8044620Z     228.     impactguard_cmd = "impactguard"  # Assume it's in PATH
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8045222Z     229. 
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8045556Z     230.     # Install pre-commit hook
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8046249Z     231.     if install_pre:
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8046748Z     232.         pre_commit_path = hooks_dir / "pre-commit"
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8047368Z     233.         pre_commit_content = rf"""#!/bin/sh>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8047941Z     234. # Pre-commit hook for ImpactGuard>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8049440Z     235. # Runs signature extraction before commit>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8050016Z     236. 
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8050671Z     237. # Extract signatures from staged Python files>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8051465Z     238. files=$(git diff --cached --name-only --diff-filter=ACM | grep '\.py$')>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8052406Z     239. if [ -n "$files" ]; then>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8053032Z     240.     echo "ImpactGuard: Extracting signatures...">
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8053747Z     241.     $impactguard_cmd extract $files > /tmp/staged_sigs.json>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8054368Z     242. fi>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8054679Z     243. 
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8054984Z     244. exit 0>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8055313Z     245. """
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8055746Z     246.         pre_commit_path.write_text(pre_commit_content)
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8056801Z     247.         os.chmod(pre_commit_path, os.stat(pre_commit_path).st_mode | stat.S_IEXEC)
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8057727Z     248.         print(f"Installed pre-commit hook: {pre_commit_path}")
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8058348Z     249. 
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8058691Z     250.     # Install post-commit hook
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8059183Z     251.     if install_post:
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8059684Z     252.         post_commit_path = hooks_dir / "post-commit"
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8060611Z     253.         post_commit_path.write_text(rf"""#!/bin/sh>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8061153Z     254. 
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8061513Z     255. # Post-commit hook for ImpactGuard>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8062091Z     256. # Ensures signature tracking is up to date>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8062621Z     257. 
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8062953Z     258. # Skip if called from hook itself>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8063463Z     259. if [ "$SKIP_SIGNATURE_HOOK" = "1" ]; then>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8063957Z     260.     exit 0>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8064356Z     261. fi>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8064685Z     262. 
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8065029Z     263. # Check if Python files changed>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8065857Z     264. changed=$(git diff-tree --no-commit-id --name-only -r HEAD | grep '\.py$' || echo "")>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8066889Z     265. 
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8067437Z     266. if [ -n "$changed" ]; then>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8068047Z     267.     echo "ImpactGuard: Updating signature tracking...">
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8068640Z     268.     
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8069048Z     269.     # Extract signatures from all Python files>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8069933Z     270.     $impactguard_cmd extract $(git ls-files | grep '\.py$') > /tmp/impactguard_sigs_$$.json>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8070763Z     271.     
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8071304Z     272.     # You can optionally commit the signatures or just keep them local>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8072152Z     273.     # For now, we just ensure the extraction runs successfully>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8072780Z     274.     if [ $? -eq 0 ]; then>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8073384Z     275.         echo "ImpactGuard: Signatures extracted successfully">
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8074017Z     276.     else>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8074539Z     277.         echo "ImpactGuard: Warning - signature extraction failed">
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8075182Z     278.     fi>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8075513Z     279. fi>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8075817Z     280. 
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8076320Z     281. exit 0>
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8076656Z     282. """)
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8077260Z     283.         os.chmod(post_commit_path, os.stat(post_commit_path).st_mode | stat.S_IEXEC)
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8078219Z     284.         print(f"Installed post-commit hook: {post_commit_path}")
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8078832Z     285. 
2026-05-05T12:14:06.8079290Z     286.     print(f"\nHooks installed successfully to {hooks_dir}")

2026-05-05T12:14:18.1355215Z     8. [![Ruff](https://img.shields.io/endpoint?url=https://raw.githubusercontent.com/astral-sh/ruff/main/assets/badge/v2.json)](https://github.com/astral-sh/ruff)
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1356684Z     9. [![Ask DeepWiki](https://deepwiki.com/badge.svg)](https://deepwiki.com/daedalus/ImpactGuard)
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1357183Z     10. 
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1357361Z     11. ## Overview
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1357551Z     12. 
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1359497Z     13. ImpactGuard is a lightweight API impact analyzer for Python projects designed to maintain API stability by tracking function signatures across commits, detecting breaking changes, and analyzing call-site impact using both static and runtime techniques.
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1360941Z     14. 
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1361481Z     15. It provides a quantitative risk framework to help developers understand the consequences of code changes before they are merged.
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1362397Z     16. 
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1362593Z     17. ### Core Capabilities
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1362825Z     18. 
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1363348Z     19. - **AST-based Extraction**: Automatically extracts function signatures, including `async def`, decorators, and type hints
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1364490Z     20. - **Semantic API Diffing**: Classifies changes into a taxonomy of breaking (e.g., removing positional arguments) vs. non-breaking (e.g., adding optional keyword-only arguments)
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1365706Z     21. - **Impact Analysis**: Correlates signature changes with static call-site extraction and optional runtime tracing to identify affected downstream code
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1366961Z     22. - **Risk Assessment**: Quantifies the danger of a change using the **S × E × C** (Severity × Exposure × Confidence) model
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1367801Z     23. - **Automated Remediation**: Generates format-preserving patches using LibCST to fix broken call sites
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1368320Z     24. 
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1368506Z     25. ### System Components
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1368735Z     26. 
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1368939Z     27. | Component | Module | Description |
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1369243Z     28. |-----------|--------|-------------|
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1369730Z     29. | Signature Extraction | `extract_signatures.py` | AST-based extraction of function metadata |
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1370420Z     30. | Signature Comparison | `compare_signatures.py` | Semantic diffing of API changes |
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1371166Z     31. | Call-Site Analysis | `extract_calls.py`, `analyze_module.py` | Static call-site extraction and resolution |
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1371843Z     32. | Impact Analysis | `impact_analysis.py` | Correlates changes with call sites |
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1372389Z     33. | Risk Model | `risk_model.py` | S × E × C risk scoring |
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1372833Z     34. | Risk Gate | `risk_gate.py`, `enforce_gate.py` | CI enforcement engine |
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1373429Z     35. | Runtime Tracing | `trace_calls.py`, `trace_calls_prod.py` | Development and production tracers |
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1374125Z     36. | Patch Generation | `cst_patch.py`, `patch_generator.py` | Format-preserving automated fixes |
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1374712Z     37. | Reporting | `generate_report.py` | Static HTML report generation |
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1375135Z     38. | CLI | `cli.py` | Command-line interface |
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1375593Z     39. 
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1375763Z     40. ---
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1376059Z     41.

2026-05-05T12:14:18.1398919Z     3. ) -> float:

2026-05-05T12:14:18.1403983Z     23.     elif name_only_match:

2026-05-05T12:14:18.1404444Z     25.     else:

2026-05-05T12:14:18.1405289Z     29. def get_structural_safety(change_type: str) -> float:
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1405761Z     30.     if "default" in change_type.lower() or "optional" in change_type.lower():
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1406414Z     31.         return 1.0
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1406688Z     32.     elif "kwarg" in change_type.lower():
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1406979Z     33.         return 0.8
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1407247Z     34.     elif "positional" in change_type.lower():
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1407553Z     35.         return 0.3
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1407777Z     36.     return 0.5
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1407981Z     37. 
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1408149Z     38. 
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1408383Z     39. def get_semantic_risk(change_type: str) -> float:
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1408735Z     40.     if "required" in change_type.lower():
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1409025Z     41.         return 0.6
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1409240Z     42.     return 1.0
2026-05-05T12:14:18.1409441Z     43.

2026-05-05T12:22:33.9479144Z       3. Push to `master` and create a GitHub Release

2026-05-05T12:22:33.9480889Z       
2026-05-05T12:22:33.9481385Z       ## Adding Change-Type Detectors
2026-05-05T12:22:33.9481990Z       
2026-05-05T12:22:33.9482708Z       Change detection lives in `compare_signatures.py`. To add a new change type:
2026-05-05T12:22:33.9483579Z       
2026-05-05T12:22:33.9484106Z       1. Add detection logic in `compare()` function
2026-05-05T12:22:33.9485050Z       2. Add the new change type key to `SEVERITY_SCORES` in `risk_model.py`
2026-05-05T12:22:33.9486121Z       3. Add tests in `tests/`
2026-05-05T12:22:33.9486762Z

I'm looking at how the test checks for severity matches—it's searching for whether the key string appears within the change type string, but I need to verify the direction of that containment check since "REQUIRED" would be found inside "REQUIRED POSITIONAL ADDED" but not the other way around.
